Sheng County

Rampant Banditry in Sheng County

Sheng County is a mountainous area and has always been plagued by bandits. On the 24th of this month, a group of more than forty bandits suddenly appeared near the 28th capital in the western countryside. The bandits were all wearing incomplete military uniforms and carrying wooden-cased guns. They first rushed into the village militia, looting four quick-firing guns and killing and injuring four soldiers. They also robbed Zhang Boqi, the former commander of the Zhenhai Fortress, of four self-defense guns and thousands of yuan worth of gold and silver jewelry. It is reported that the number of bandits has recently gathered to more than two hundred, and they have stormed into more than ten villages in the four districts. The scale of the banditry is unprecedented. Furthermore, according to news from Shaoxing, the military and police have dispatched teams to Sheng County to defend against the rampant bandits. The villages bordering the area are especially panicked. Tangpu Township also had a false alarm the other day. Sun Zhusheng, the village head of Sunkan Village in Tangpu Township, Sheng County, recently received a home report while shopping in Tangpu Market, saying that a bandit letter had arrived, stating that the army (the bandits' self-proclaimed name) would pass through the area on the 1st and requesting that 200 tables of lunch be prepared. As soon as this news spread, the people in the villages near Sunkan and Tangpu were panic-stricken, and some even fled to other places. Fortunately, nothing happened on the 1st, but they had already suffered a false alarm.

Special Report

The Opinion Letter on Tax Revenue Policy from the Ministry of Finance's Gamel Design Committee (Continued)

The impact on tax revenue of reducing the types of taxes will not necessarily have an adverse impact on revenue. After the number of taxes is reduced, even if it is necessary to increase the tax rate on certain items that are deemed to still require taxation, the tax can be levied on special items that can bear a high tax rate. On the one hand, those who pay other types of taxes can be exempted. This reform is easy to implement. However, it should be noted that the increase in the tax rate should not be carried out rashly. The impact of the tax rate increase on the commodity market must be carefully considered because the state's income is closely related to this impact. Moreover, reducing the number of taxes is also sufficient to increase net income, because simple taxes can save administrative costs. The problem of China's tax administration will be discussed in detail later.

If the above arguments are appropriate, then it is not necessary to seek alternative taxes for those that have already been abolished. However, because there may be occasional errors in determining the tax rate and removing certain items from the tax table, which will be detrimental to finance, in order to avoid this adverse effect, it is not unmanageable to stipulate alternative taxes as a preventive and temporary measure. However, in general, if the aforementioned reform methods can be gradual, then alternative taxes are not necessary.

A Balanced Tax System

After discussing the impact of the tax system on trade and commerce, the following will focus on whether the tax burden is balanced for people of all classes, even if they are not necessarily direct taxpayers, but are ultimately the ones who bear the tax burden.

Most of the taxes currently collected by the national government are borne by consumers of taxable goods. Some people consider this distribution of the tax burden satisfactory, while others believe that the satisfaction of taxes must depend on whether the distribution of the tax burden is in accordance with the people's ability to pay. Many national legislators often say that countries like China, which rely mainly on taxes on goods, should correct or supplement their tax system with direct taxes such as income tax and inheritance tax.

In a memorandum on income tax submitted on September 4, 1929, this committee suggested that China should not adopt a set income tax at the present time. Subsequently, further research on special or partial income tax did not prove that this limited income tax was suitable for adoption. The committee's view is based partly on the nature of income, partly on the current state of Chinese private accounts, and mainly on the administrative nature. Once the conditions that other countries consider suitable for income tax are also seen in China, then China can certainly adopt income tax, but it must still be local and experimental at first.

The committee also believes that China should not adopt an inheritance tax at the present time for similar reasons. This type of tax is based on the family property and inheritance of Western countries, but the situation in China is not the same. The orphans of deceased parents, whether their degree of dependence on this property or their management and use of this property, their status does not change due to the death of their parents. In European and Western countries, the usual reason for collecting inheritance tax is that the inheritors suddenly increase their industry, and their ability to subsidize the country naturally increases, so they can be levied an inheritance tax. However, there is no such stable situation in China, even if there is, it is only a very small number.

Although there is little data on this point, it is sufficient to prove that China's concepts, habits, and industrial registration system regarding families and industries are different from those of Western countries. Even if China implements the collection of inheritance tax today, it will not be very effective.

In addition to the above two types of direct taxes, there is another type of direct tax, namely land tax, which should be discussed. It is appropriate for this stable tax to be collected by local governments, but in fact, the central government of many countries receives a portion of the land tax revenue. The two points regarding land registration and natural appreciation of land tax will be described separately below.

China has never had an appropriate system for registering property rights on land, and there is no precise method for dividing boundaries. To reform this malpractice, it is necessary to measure the land of the whole country, but in view of the current financial situation, this is impossible. However, this work can be carried out gradually, under national supervision, starting first with one or several provinces or several parts of a province.

A clear registration of land industry can be established based on the results of this measurement to achieve the purpose of taxation. At the same time, the taxable value of the industry should be estimated in order to correct the existing land registers, which were mostly made centuries ago and contain many unfair aspects.

At present, most counties and cities in China are expanding and improving public facilities, especially in the national capital. This improvement is sufficient to increase the value of the industry. It is fair for the government to extract a considerable portion of the increased value of this private industry as an improvement cost or part of its cost. The amount of compensation given to private industries for damages caused by municipal improvements should also be part of the aforementioned costs. It does not seem appropriate to discuss the applicable methods of this so-called natural appreciation tax in detail here. In China, the already returned German leased territory of Jiaozhou (Qingdao) is a precedent for this tax. Also, the application of this tax in Guangdong Province was discussed several years ago. This committee believes that the methods and effects of the aforementioned cases should be studied to adopt similar taxes where the situation permits. (To be continued)

Educational News Highlights

Ministry of Education Orders Universities to Abolish Vice-Presidents

The Executive Yuan, upon receiving the resignation request from Dai Chuanxian, President of Zhongshan University, and proposing that Zhu Jiahua be the president and Shen Hongfei be the vice-president, was forwarded by the Yuan to the National Government for review. Subsequently, at the 93rd State Council meeting, it was resolved to approve the president's resignation and appoint Vice-President Zhu Jiahua as the president. Because the university organization law does not provide for the establishment of vice-presidents, it was resolved that there was no need to establish another vice-president. The university was ordered to amend its regulations in accordance with the university organization law, and the Ministry of Education was notified. It is learned that after receiving the order, the Ministry of Education has now informed all universities that they must comply with the order in accordance with the university organization law. If vice-presidents have already been established, they should immediately comply with the order to abolish them and amend the university's regulations.

Ministry of Education Issues Questionnaire on Moral Education Materials for Primary and Secondary Schools

The Ministry of Education previously planned to draft standards for moral education in primary and secondary schools and has issued a general order to collect relevant materials. Educational bureaus of various provinces and cities have successively submitted reports to the Ministry of Education. The Ministry believes that objective evidence should support these standards and that thorough investigation and research should be conducted before drafting can begin. To gather diverse perspectives, the Ministry has now created a questionnaire on moral education materials for primary and secondary schools, which is distributed to educational bureaus in various provinces and cities. It is hoped that staff with experience and knowledge in primary and secondary school moral education will gather to fill out one questionnaire. Additionally, it is hoped that the questionnaire will be distributed to urban or rural primary and secondary schools under their jurisdiction with outstanding performance for completion and submission to the Ministry within one month. The questionnaire on moral education materials for primary and secondary schools includes the following eight categories of questions: (1 & 2) What are the common good habits of primary and secondary school students? What are the bad habits? (3) What are the most effective specific methods for developing good habits and overcoming bad habits? (4 & 5) In observing students' character and behavior, what are the advantages and disadvantages that belong to the national character of our country? (6) In observing students' character and behavior, what are the advantages that our national character lacks but other national characters possess? (7) What materials from the teachings of Sun Yat-sen can serve as moral education standards? (8) Please attach any moral education standards and outlines you have seen or personally experienced and submit them to the Ministry with your opinions.

Local News

City Scout Council Election Tomorrow

The Shanghai Boy Scouts Council election, organized by the Training Department of the Municipal Party Headquarters, will be held at 1 p.m. tomorrow (the 5th) on the third floor of the Municipal Party Headquarters. Preparations for all matters are complete. According to the organizational regulations, the city has seven directors. In addition to the director of the Training Department and the director of the Education Bureau who are ex-officio directors, the remaining five directors and three alternates will be elected by mutual vote of the service personnel. It has been verified that there are ninety-four service personnel with the right to vote and be elected. A public notice has been posted in the newspaper. It is reported that six people have withdrawn: Ren Errong, Zheng Baoshan, Li Zhihua, Li Jinji, Gong Xiu'e, and Zhang Shifang. Six people have registered: Jiang Xiulin, Hu Yuru, Zhu Zhijing, Zhang Chuan Dao, Huang Zhihong, and Wu Chuliang. The total number remains ninety-four. The newly registered service personnel who have not been notified are still allowed to participate in the election at that time. Those who register later will not be allowed to vote according to the department's first announcement and need not attend. The city council election rules are copied below:

China Boy Scouts, County and City Council Member Election Rules (Issued by the Headquarters of the China Boy Scouts) (Article 1) These rules apply when electing council members of the county and city councils of the China Boy Scouts, in accordance with the organizational regulations of the county and city councils of the China Boy Scouts. (Article 2) The election of council members of the county and city councils of the China Boy Scouts is organized by the previous council election meeting; in counties and cities without a council, it is organized by the training department of the county and city party headquarters. (Article 3) The convocation of the council election meeting of the China Boy Scouts county and city councils must issue a notice half a month in advance. (Article 4) The council election meeting of the China Boy Scouts county and city councils must have more than one-half of the China Boy Scouts service personnel in the entire county and city present to be held. (Article 5) The right to vote and be elected as a council member of the China Boy Scouts county and city councils is limited to those who hold a China Boy Scouts service personnel certificate and have resided in the respective county or city for more than one month. (Article 6) The election of council members of the China Boy Scouts county and city councils uses a joint-name voting method. (Article 7) The ballots are created by the Headquarters of the China Boy Scouts and handed over to the council of each province to send personnel to distribute them on the spot. However, before the council of the province is established, it is handed over to the training department of the party headquarters of the province for distribution. (Article 8) When voters arrive at the election site, they must wear Boy Scout uniforms and present their China Boy Scouts service personnel certificates to receive the ballot. (Article 9) The ballot must be filled out and cast into the ballot box by the voter in person. (Article 10) During the election, a supervisor designated by a higher-level organization must be present to supervise the election for it to be valid. (Article 11) The election of council members of the China Boy Scouts county and city councils is based on the number of votes received. Those with more votes are elected, and those with the next highest number of votes are alternates. If the number of votes is the same, the decision is made by drawing lots. (Article 12) The supervisor must count the ballots immediately after the election is completed. (Article 13) If the ballot has any of the following circumstances, it will be invalid as a whole ballot: 1. It is not filled out according to the format or other words are written on it. 2. All handwriting is blurry and cannot be recognized. 3. The voter has not signed or the signature does not match the name on their service personnel certificate. (Article 14) If the ballot has any of the following circumstances, it will be partially invalid: 1. The filled-in candidate does not comply with the provisions of Article 5. 2. The name of the filled-in candidate does not match the name on the candidate's service personnel certificate. 3. The handwriting of the name of the filled-in candidate is blurry and cannot be recognized. (Article 15) The supervisor will decide and execute the invalidity of the entire ballot or part of the ballot. (Article 16) After the election, the organizing agency, together with the supervisor, will report the election results, along with the ballots, to be filed in accordance with the law. (Article 17) The election of council members of the China Boy Scouts Council in cities directly under the Executive Yuan shall apply mutatis mutandis to the provisions of these rules. (Article 18) These rules are promulgated and implemented by the Headquarters of the China Boy Scouts.

|Friendship Games|

Expeditionary Soccer Team Returns to Shanghai Yesterday

｜Yu Hengzhi and Seven Others Returned to Shanghai Yesterday｜Li Huitang is in Hong Kong｜

Welcome of Relatives and Friends Arriving in Port

The Chinese Expeditionary Soccer Team, organized by the Lehua Sports Association, returned to Shanghai yesterday morning at 11:00 aboard the French postal ship Porthos, after being abroad for three months. Relatives and friends at sea flocked to the China Merchants General Wharf to welcome them as scheduled. Qiu Feihai, Rong Qizhao, Guang Daozhang, Wu Bangwei, Wang Fudan, Wei Zexian, Li Silian and others were also among them. Suddenly, the ship was in sight, and the team leader, Yu Hengzhi, and others waved to each other. Soon, old friends reunited, talking and laughing. Sun Sijing, Zhou Xianyan, Feng Yun Gu, An Yuansheng, Dai Linjing, Chen Yutian, Chen Jiaqiu, and Zhang Xulong came with the ship. At 2:00 pm, the reporter met Yu Hengzhi again at the Guangdong Club. The reporter asked about the truth of the expedition's termination, the issue of participating in various Westerners Association competitions, and the future progress of Lehua. The points made by Yu Jun are detailed below.

The Truth About the Termination of the Expedition

The plan to expedition to Europe and America had been in preparation for a long time. Later, it was taken over by Li Silian on his return to China. The outline had been determined, so Lehua began to collect players. In addition to the basic players of the team, it was originally planned to invite players from South China and Singapore to join, forming a team. Unexpectedly, the Hong Kong Football Association denied the addition of South China players in response to inquiries from London. The ambitious plan for the expedition was terminated. The sudden departure and stop of the South China players were actually due to the Hong Kong Chinese and South China Sports Associations. The only way to maintain the association's economy was to rely on the income from the football season. If the famous generals were to leave, the ability to call would be diminished, and the association's affairs would inevitably be hindered, so they had to find a way to obstruct it. It was not selfish, but forced by the environment. However, the Chinese Expeditionary Soccer Team suffered all kinds of blows, resulting in failure.

Participating in Westerners Association Competitions

Yu Jun said that Lehua is a member of the Westerners Association and should not be given the assumption of a false word suddenly without prior notice. A letter will be sent to inquire and ask for an explanation of the reason for the suspicion. Before replying, a wait-and-see attitude will be adopted. If a satisfactory reply cannot be obtained, it will be better to sacrifice and withdraw.

Lehua's Future Progress

Yu Jun did not have a clear answer to the question of Lehua's future progress, but said that he would wait for the discussion of the association's board of directors. Currently, the team members Dai Linjing, Chen Zhenhe, Feng Yun You, Chen Jiaqiu, and Jiang Shanjing will all serve their alma mater. Those who can serve the team are Zhou Xianyan, Sun Sijing, Li Huitang, An Yuansheng, and Chen Yutian. Li is now in Hong Kong and is scheduled to come to Shanghai on the 9th. Li Ning has returned to his hometown of Shatou, and it is unknown when he will come. Sun Sijing took the Fu Sheng Hao back to Tianjin last night and will return to Shanghai in ten days. Zhang Xiyun, a famous defender from Singapore, is temporarily staying in Shanghai to replace him in his work. According to his statement, if Lehua reorganizes, it will inevitably seek new talent.

Lehua Will Publish the Process

Finally, Yu Jun said that the board of directors will publish the process and economic situation of this expedition in the near future. Yu Jun himself will also disclose the details of the termination of the expedition so that the world will not have any doubts.

The Battle Record of the Nanyang Islands

During this Chinese Expeditionary Soccer Team's expedition to the Nanyang Islands, they achieved remarkable results in the east and west. A total of twenty-three matches were played, including twelve in Java, three in Saigon, three in Singapore, four in Medan, and one in Kuala Lumpur. There were thirteen wins, six draws, and four losses. A total of sixty goals were scored and thirty-four goals were conceded. Personal achievements: Huitang 24, Linjing 18, Guicheng 6, Yutian 5, Jiaqiu 3, Guangyao 3, and Sijing 1.

Total Victory in Saigon

September 23rd Victory over the All-Vietnam Team Eight to One

September 24th Victory over the Saigon Champions Three to Zero

September 25th Victory over the Six Provinces Elite Three to One

The above three battles are the expeditionary force's proudest works, and also the last three of the expedition. Every player recovered their health and had good performances. In the first battle, they defeated the All-Vietnam team by eight to one. Li Huitang scored four goals, Dai Linjing scored one goal, Cao Guicheng scored two goals, and Chen Guangyao scored one goal. In the second battle, they defeated the Saigon champions by three to zero. Huitang scored two goals and Guicheng scored one goal. In the last group, Huitang, Guicheng, and Yutian each scored one goal.

Zhang Xueliang Sends Personnel to Prepare for the North China Games

Shenyang Communication. The North China Games this year were originally scheduled to be held in Jinan or Tianjin, but due to the current situation, the Preparatory Committee announced the suspension. Zhang Xueliang heard about this and did not want the China Games to fail after the failure of the Far East Games, believing that it would expose the weakness of the country too much. He ordered the Preparatory Committee member Hao Gengsheng to organize it in Shenyang. Later, because the province was preparing for the Northeast Four Provinces Joint Games, which was approaching, it was difficult to take care of the China Games at the same time in terms of time and preparation, so it was decided not to hold it. Recently, Zhang Xueliang decided that since the Northeast Army had occupied Tianjin and Beijing and the North China territory had returned to the Northeast, the China Games would still be continued during this period. On the 29th, it was decided that Liu Fengzhu, Wang Zhaofan, Sun Guofeng, Li Shutang, Wu Jiaxiang, Feng Yong, Wang Jiexian, Li Jingcheng, Li Xianggeng, Ji Zhenduo, Hao Gengsheng, Wang Huayi, Wang Zhuoran, Hang, Ning Encheng, etc., would be the Liaison Committee members in Liaoning for the Preparatory Committee of the North China Games. Each committee member has scheduled to meet at the Provincial Education Association on the afternoon of the 30th to discuss all preparations. However, this Northeast Four Provinces Joint Games is an innovation in the Northeast and has been in preparation for many days. If the China Games are prepared at the same time, there will be many inconveniences in fact. It is heard that the relevant parties have decided that all athletes from various places who should participate in the China Games will be invited by the Four Provinces Joint Games to join the Joint Games and will no longer hold a separate China Games after the event.

Various Circles Prepare for National Day Commemoration

Various Circles in the Third District: The Preparatory Committee for the Celebration of National Day by various circles in the Third District of this city held its second preparatory committee meeting yesterday at the Caojiadu Defense Corps. Tang Liqing was publicly elected as chairman. The meeting proceeded with formalities. The chairman reported on the execution of resolutions from the previous session, and then discussions began: (1) Regarding the proposal to appoint the duties of newly appointed committee members, it was resolved that all should be appointed as Deputy Directors of the Finance Department, and Ma Yusheng and Yu Yuqing should also serve as Deputy Directors of the Lantern Department. (2) Regarding the location and expenses for the dinner, it was resolved that (a) the location would be decided next time, (b) the cost would be two yuan per person, and (c) the deadline for registration would be October 8th. (3) The Lantern Department proposed a draft of Lantern Guidelines for review and approval, which was resolved to be amended and passed. (4) The Entertainment Department proposed that the entertainment expenses in Caojiadu would be the responsibility of Li Meiqing, Director of Finance in Caojiadu, and those in the Municipal Chamber of Commerce would be the responsibility of the Third District Party Headquarters, which was resolved and passed. (5) Regarding the proposal to appoint the Presidium for the celebration ceremony, it was resolved to appoint Tang Liqing, Duan Shaozhong, Ren Lvping, Li Meiqing, Yao Yuguan, Zhou Shangen, and Yang Shaozhi as members of the Presidium. (6) Regarding the proposal to appoint the Master of Ceremonies for the celebration ceremony, it was resolved to appoint Zhang Yongkang as the Master of Ceremonies. (7) Regarding the proposal to appoint the Chief and Deputy Commanders and Chief and Deputy Disciplinarians for the lantern parade, it was resolved that Jin Fuchun would be the Chief Commander, Zhou Shangen would be the Chief Disciplinarian, Zhu Rongping would be the Deputy Commander, and Yang Chen would be the Deputy Disciplinarian. (8) Regarding the proposal to determine the route for the lantern parade, it was resolved that the Lantern Department would determine the route and submit it to the next general meeting for discussion. (9) Regarding the proposal to determine the location of the office, it was resolved to have two locations: (1) the Third District Party Headquarters, and (2) the Caojiadu Defense Corps. (10) Regarding the proposal to determine the date of the next meeting, it was resolved to be at 3:00 PM on October 7th at the Caojiadu Defense Corps.

Various Circles in West Shanghai: The Fifth Branch of the Ninth District of the city convened various organizations in the Fahua area to hold a preparatory meeting for the National Day commemoration. Yang Shuchun, a standing committee member, was publicly elected as chairman, and Xu Jiying, a propaganda committee member, served as the recorder. (1) The meeting proceeded with formalities. (2) The chairman reported on the significance of preparing for the National Day commemoration. (3) It was resolved that: (1) A large-scale celebration would be held at Guanghua University on National Day. (2) All groups would gather to hold a lantern parade. (3) Teams would march to promote the significance of National Day to the public. (4) Order would be maintained by armed police officers dispatched by the Public Security Bureau. (5) Comrade Yang Shuchun was publicly elected as chairman of the assembly and would report on the significance of National Day and the public's awareness and efforts. (6) Yang Shuchun, a municipal affairs commissioner, and Comrade Xu Jiying were publicly elected as chief commanders.

Various Circles in Jiangwan: The Jiangwan Public Celebration of National Day Preparatory Committee held its second preparatory meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday. Shen Zurui was publicly elected as chairman. The meeting proceeded with formalities. After the chairman and various departments reported, the following was discussed: (1) How should the assembly point for the lantern parade be decorated? It was resolved that: 1. A large archway would be erected at the entrance of the relief society, to be handled by the Shanghai Municipal Council. 2. Colored lights would be installed around and on top of the Sun Yat-sen Memorial. 3. A general command platform would be set up in front of the Laoda Auditorium. 4. Three tea service points would be set up at the assembly point. (2) Regarding the proposal to hold various gatherings in stages, it was resolved to proceed as previously resolved, except that elementary school students participating in the entertainment performances could opt out of the lantern parade. (3) Regarding the proposal to re-specify the time and location for the celebration and entertainment events, it was resolved that the celebration would be held at 1:30 PM on October 10th, and the entertainment would begin at 2:00 PM in the new auditorium of Labor University. (4) Regarding the proposal to specify the assembly point and departure time for the lantern parade, it was resolved that the Jiangwan contingent would assemble at the entrance of Laoda at 6:00 PM on the 10th, and the Yinxiang Port contingent would depart from the Sanyou Trade Union at 6:00 PM on the 9th. (5) How should the entertainment stage be decorated? It was resolved that the Entertainment Department would be responsible. (6) Regarding the proposal to specify the publicity materials to be printed, it was resolved to produce a special issue in the size of a daily newspaper, 1,000 leaflets, and 1,000 red and green paper slogans, to be handled by the Propaganda Department. (7) Regarding the proposal to use cargo trucks to transport all the heavy lanterns and decorations after the lantern parade, it was resolved to subsidize the transportation fee of 12 yuan. (8) Regarding the proposal to invite the Yinxing Defense Corps to participate in National Day and maintain local security, it was resolved to pass and hand it over to the General Affairs Department for handling. (9) Regarding the proposal to request the removal of all awnings and obstacles on the streets during the lantern parade, it was resolved to send a letter to the Public Security Bureau for handling. (10) Regarding the proposal that all shops and organizations should hang national flags and festive lanterns on National Day, it was resolved to pass and hand it over to the General Affairs Department for handling. (11) Regarding the date of the next meeting, it was resolved to be at 2:00 PM on the 7th of this month. The meeting adjourned.

Reception for Diplomatic Missions: The Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs received a telegram from the Ministry stating that the Ministry would hold a tea party on October 10th, National Day, to receive the diplomatic envoys and representatives of various countries in China to mark the celebration. In addition to notifying Minister Odenko, leader of the diplomatic missions in Beijing, it also instructed the Shanghai Office to notify the consulates and representative offices of various countries in Shanghai to prepare a list of names for participation in Beijing and prepare for reception. The Shanghai Office yesterday sent letters to nine countries, including Norwegian Minister Aubert, Cuban Minister Piedra, Belgian Minister Wallers, Japanese Chargé d'Affaires Shigemitsu, Turkish Chargé d'Affaires Ford Bey, Finnish Chargé d'Affaires Vamelyki, Polish Chargé d'Affaires Wedentaw, Czech Representative Ni Ci Yu, and the representative office of the British Minister in Shanghai, requesting them to provide lists for submission to the Ministry for reception.

Municipal Government Plans to Establish Grain Storage

The Bureau of Social Affairs forwarded to the Municipal Government for approval the fact that this year's rice harvest is abundant and the new rice is coming onto the market, which will inevitably lead to a surge in supply. At that time, the price of rice will inevitably fall. Currently, the new rice has not yet flooded the market, and the price of rice has already fallen to about sixteen yuan. According to the observations of most people, there is still the possibility of further decline. People are generally happy to hear that grain is cheap, but they do not know that when new grain comes out, the price of rice is too low, which is also harmful. At a time when everything is expensive, farmers cannot make ends meet. In the coming year, rice cultivation will inevitably switch to more profitable crops, which will reduce grain production. When unscrupulous merchants see that the price of rice is low, they believe that there is no profit to be made domestically, and they often smuggle it abroad to raise the domestic grain price. The result is almost the same as forming a situation where expensive rice is imported in famine years and cheap rice is exported in bumper years. The only way to remedy this is to immediately raise huge sums of money to be purchased by the government when rice is cheap to regulate the market and keep prices balanced. This is the only way to resist the cunning schemes of unscrupulous merchants to destroy the people's food supply and ensure long-term food security. It is reported that the Bureau of Social Affairs received instructions from the Municipal Government to approve the consultation of the Ministry of the Interior and the order of the Executive Yuan. At the 242nd meeting of the Central Political Conference, Committee Member Chen Guofu proposed a plan to establish grain storage and ordered that it be examined and reported. According to the resolution of the Food Committee, the funds for grain storage in counties and cities should be divided and a fund of one million yuan should be raised to handle grain storage. The Municipal Government was requested to first organize a fundraising committee for the warehouse fund and raise one million yuan within three months. This is because the city has a large population and requires a large amount of food. The original warehouses have long been rebuilt into civilian houses and rented out. The funds for grain storage over the years have also been insufficient. Moreover, it is jointly managed by the city and county, and has not yet been divided. Now, for the sake of storing up for famine relief, it is necessary to raise ample funds. The city's famine relief fund of 200,000 yuan has been finalized, but due to the city's financial difficulties, it must be allocated within ten years, which is a drop in the bucket and difficult to help. Therefore, the Bureau of Social Affairs has made this proposal.

Municipal Government Bans Old Calendars

The Municipal Government, considering that recently peddlers in the concessions have been hawking old calendars from the twentieth year of the Republic, hindering the promotion of the national calendar, has specially requested the Special District Local Court to instruct the Public Works Department of the Bureau to strictly prohibit such sales. The original letter stated, "Regarding the letter No. 1396 from the Secretariat of the Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang, stating that the Third District Party Department under the committee requested that the Municipal Government be consulted to negotiate with the concession authorities to ban peddlers from hawking old calendars from the twentieth year of the Republic to uphold the law, etc., which has been submitted and approved by the Standing Committee and forwarded to the Municipal Government, etc., accordingly, we are enclosing a copy of the submission and sending it to your esteemed government for review and handling, and a reply is requested." It is understood that unscrupulous merchants are privately printing old calendars in the concessions and enticing peddlers to hawk them along the streets, which is a violation of the prohibition and should be strictly prohibited. In addition to replying to the letter, we are enclosing a copy of the submission and sending it to your esteemed court to instruct the Public Works Department of the Bureau to investigate and handle, and a reply is requested.

Weihaiwei Postal Service Now Taken Over by Chinese Postal Service

Beginning on the second of this month, according to the Shanghai Postal Authority, the postal affairs of Weihaiwei have been taken over by the Chinese Postal Service starting on the second of this month. In the future, mail and packages sent to that area will be charged according to domestic rates and handled according to domestic postal regulations.

Overseas Chinese Federation's Methods to Assist in the Xiao Case

Telegram Calling on All Circles to Unite and Rise Up

Boycott the Java Shipping Company

The Overseas Chinese Federation yesterday telegraphed to party departments at all levels, governments at all levels, newspapers, organizations, support associations for the Xiao case in various ports, the Yixing Shanghai Alumni Association, and the Nanjing Central District Experimental School, stating that the chief mate and second mate of the Java Shipping Company's ship Tjibadak forcibly defiled Ms. Xiao Xin'an, a Chinese female teacher, and more than a month has passed, and the humiliation has not been avenged. For the honor of the entire nation, for the dignity of the entire country, for the personality of all female compatriots, and for the dignity of female teachers, our association must loudly appeal to compatriots at home and abroad to urgently provide assistance. In addition to urging the diplomatic authorities to seriously negotiate, it is urgent to unite and rise up to boycott all ships of the Java Shipping Company (Java　Chin

aJapanLuyn) as a diplomatic backing. We will never stop until the chief mate and second mate of the Tjibadak are severely punished, the Dutch government officially apologizes to our nation, and Ms. Xiao receives reasonable compensation. The chief mate and second mate dared to indulge in bestial desires towards Ms. Xiao because they no longer recognized the Chinese as human beings. Therefore, they did not dare to approach Europeans and Japanese, but went straight to Ms. Xiao, who was unfortunately born a Chinese, thinking that the Chinese are a lowly race, with no sense of national honor, lacking national consciousness, pursuing selfishness, and embracing individualism as the public creed of lowly Chinese. Who would be willing to lift a finger to help if Ms. Xiao was insulted? Therefore, they dared to call their kind and force Ms. Xiao to commit suicide by taking poison again and again. Our association does not recognize that the Chinese have such inferior nature and deeply wishes to follow all circles to avenge this strange humiliation of being looked down upon and forcibly defiled. Who does not have a wife and daughter? Who would willingly suffer humiliation? If we do not help the Xiao case, how can we know that the next person defiled will not be our own wife and daughter? Helping Xiao is helping ourselves, helping others is helping ourselves. Municipal Government Prepares to Receive American Far East Economic Survey Mission

The mission is expected to arrive in Shanghai around November 30th. The British Far East Economic Survey Mission is currently led by Sir Thompson, former president of the Manchester Chamber of Commerce, to investigate the commercial situation of Britain in China and Japan, and the methods to promote trade. Attached is a cotton industry survey mission, which is specifically for investigating the development of the British cotton industry in the Far East and the methods to promote the industry. The survey mission is expected to arrive in Shanghai around November 30th and will conduct investigations in Shanghai and surrounding areas for about one month. They will first go to the capital to visit the National Government, and then conduct a thorough investigation in the Shanghai area. Some members of the mission will go to Hankou from Shanghai for investigation. In the second month, the mission will conduct investigations in Beiping, Tianjin, Liaoning, Harbin, Dalian, and other places. In the third month, they will conduct investigations in South China. The Municipal Government of this city yesterday received a letter from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs reporting the above news. Considering that the survey mission is organized by well-known figures in the British business community, and this visit to China to investigate the economic, commercial, and cotton industry situation of Britain in the Far East is closely related to the development of our country's international trade, the Municipal Government has ordered the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs to make proper preparations for reception.

Mayor Zhang Sends Telegram to Senior Civil Official Gu

Please Convey to Government Officials

My Desire to Resign from China Merchants Bureau Committee

Mayor Zhang Yuejun was previously appointed by the National Government as a member of the China Merchants Bureau Reorganization Committee and designated as the chairman. He respectfully telegraphed the National Government last month to resign, but subsequently received instructions from the National Government expressing deep trust and sincerely retaining him. Upon hearing the news in Shenyang, Mayor Zhang telegraphed the National Government again on the Eastern day of this month to express his resignation for the second time, with great determination, expressing that he would never take office no matter what. The content of the telegram has been seen in another article, and the wording is extremely sincere, coming from the heart, and is not a feigned modesty. Still fearing that the National Government would retain him again, he specially telegraphed Senior Civil Official Gu of the National Government Civil Affairs Office on the Winter day to express his sincerity, requesting him to convey to the government officials that his resignation should be approved as soon as possible. Here is a summary of the telegram: "Senior Civil Official Gu Xiangqin of the Civil Affairs Office of the National Government in Nanjing, the National Government has ordered me to serve concurrently as a member of the China Merchants Bureau Committee. I really do not have the ability to handle this matter concurrently, and I especially do not want one person to serve concurrently in two unrelated matters. I telegraphed to resign last month but was not approved, and instead received encouragement, which has increased my anxiety. I am telegraphing again to resign and am returning the appointment letter to Shanghai. I hope that you will convey my words to the government officials and approve my resignation as soon as possible, so that another capable person can be appointed to avoid important matters being suspended for a long time and hindering progress. If I resign again and again, it will only cause trouble and ultimately achieve nothing. I respectfully ask for your understanding. Zhang Qun kowtows on the Winter day."

"To the National Government in Nanjing, I previously heard the order to reorganize the China Merchants Bureau Committee and telegraphed to resign on the Respect day of last month. Recently, I received news from Shanghai that I respectfully reviewed the government's instructions on the Tolerance day to retain me and encourage me. I am filled with gratitude and anxiety. I think that I have dedicated myself to the party and the country and have never dared to shirk my responsibilities. I have never dared to avoid anything on the revolutionary path. However, the Shanghai Municipal Government and the China Merchants Bureau are both important matters and have their own responsibilities. I think that my talent and energy are insufficient to handle both at the same time. In all my management and planning, I am cautious of being distracted. Moreover, the position of chairman of the China Merchants Bureau Reorganization Committee is crucial and affects the future of the shipping industry. My resignation comes from sincerity, and I hope you will understand my sincere intentions. Rather than making mistakes in the future, it is better to be cautious now. Therefore, I am telegraphing again to resign, and I hope that you will approve my resignation quickly. Zhang Qun kowtows on the Eastern day."

Xiong Shihui Rectifies Military Discipline

Xiong Shihui, Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the three provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui, issued a general order yesterday to the military, police, and local defense organizations in the three provinces, stating that they must not recruit or retain soldiers from the Fifth Division in the future. If any are discovered, they must be reported or transferred to the division headquarters immediately. Otherwise, once discovered, the head of the organization will be held responsible and punished according to military law.

The Zhenru Radio Station Will Soon Be Completed

The French-built Radio Station Will Also Be Completed Soon

The Continental Daily reports that, according to an employee of the American Radio Corporation in Sassoon House, the construction of the Zhenru Radio Station will soon be completed, so that Shanghai and San Francisco can communicate by radio telegraph. The Zhenru Radio Station specializes in transmitting, and there is also a radio station in Liuhang that specializes in receiving. The two radio stations are connected by 24 pairs of lead-covered wires. The automatic mechanism for transmission and reception is controlled by the telegraph room of the Sassoon House head office. The equipment is all the latest type. The telegrams sent from Shanghai can be received in San Francisco immediately. Currently, telegrams sent from Shanghai to the United States must be routed through the Philippines, so it takes two hours to be transmitted. Now that direct communication is possible, it will only take 30 minutes, and the cost can be reduced. This project was contracted by the National Government with the American Radio Corporation, which invested in the construction of the station and undertook the operation for ten years, after which the government would own it. In addition, the French-built radio station in Zhenru, which uses French equipment, will also be completed soon and can be put into operation before the end of this year.

Further Postponement of the Jinliyuan Case Execution

Gao Shuo Visited the French Consul to Resolve the Jinliyuan Wharf Case: The deadline set by the French Consulate has passed again, but the reply from Paris has not yet arrived. General Manager Li of the China Merchants Bureau is eager to resolve this case. Yesterday, he specially invited lawyer Gao Shuo to visit the French Consul General to discuss the matter at the French Consulate for a long time in the morning. As a result, the French Consul General stated that the responsibility for the delay lies with the church and agreed to notify the Consulate General immediately that the execution would be postponed again to allow both parties to have an opportunity to consult. Mr. Gao immediately expressed his gratitude and the meeting ended satisfactorily.

Fourth Day of National Anti-Drug Week

Anti-Drug Family Day

Today is the fourth day of the Seventh National Anti-Drug Week, namely Anti-Drug Family Day. The purpose of this day is to promote women's anti-drug movement and focus on publicity in the family aspect. The situation is recorded as follows:

Anti-Drug Family Day Measures: A. Significance: Opium and drugs have a profound impact on families, destroying family finances, undermining family morality, and endangering family happiness. Various incidents are innumerable. In every country, compatriots have become addicted to opium, leading to family disintegration. It is imperative to eliminate opium and transform families first, ensuring that there are no such dregs in the house. B. Purpose: How to improve the family and avoid the scourge of opium and drugs? The primary work should be to promote health knowledge, avoid bad habits, adopt proper entertainment, and pay attention to anti-drug education. If the anti-drug wind spreads throughout the country, the scourge of opium will be fundamentally eliminated, and families will gain unlimited happiness. C. Measures: (1) Hold a family anti-drug carnival. (2) Female students give speeches and investigate the facts of family smoking disasters. (3) Organize women's anti-drug propaganda association. (4) Publish a special issue on women's anti-drug campaign. (9) Hold a grand anti-drug oath-taking ceremony for women.

Outline of Anti-Drug Family Day Propaganda

Opium is a poisonous substance that destroys the country and the people. The cruelty of floods and beasts is less than that of opium. It is the great enemy of mankind, the evil of society, and the destroyer of families, harming people's livelihood, endangering the race, and impoverishing the country and the people. Therefore, if it is not eliminated, the disasters will be endless. In recent years, the anti-drug movement has reached the clouds and shaken China and foreign countries, making the people of the country thoroughly aware and rising up together to put it out. It is very fortunate. People who are addicted to smoking are confused, do not engage in proper work, and indulge in smoking all day long. The rich become poor and eventually lose everything, their wives and children suffer from cold and hunger, their family business is destroyed, and their lives are extremely difficult. However, the smoking addiction still cannot be quit, and they become robbers and beggars. Moreover, once a smoking addiction is developed, the poison enters the bones, and the harm of fertility and inheritance is infinite. Other important issues such as family education are destroyed because of this. Even with a good wife and virtuous mother, there is nothing they can do to help, and they can only watch the happy family turn into a cruel hell. We hope that our female compatriots will think deeply and take precautions, and make a firm determination to refuse drugs and have a family. We will embrace the ambition to put out the scourge of smoking and achieve the ultimate goal of eliminating it. (1) Advocate family anti-drug movement. The sin of opium is as described above, and its scope and depth of harm have become unmanageable. Therefore, to solve this problem, it is necessary to awaken women across the country and strive to promote the family anti-drug movement. Opium poison is based in the family, where it parasitizes, breeds, grows, and spreads to all aspects of society. Therefore, the foundation of the anti-drug movement must be established in the family, so that the general mothers know the importance of anti-drug education and pay attention to their children. In their childhood, they should be taught about the harm of opium and narcotic drugs, which are the roots of bad physique, loss of intelligence, moral decline, national destruction, and racial extinction, and how to eradicate them, so that they can understand the meaning of anti-drug education early and vow not to plant, transport, sell, or use opium and all narcotic drugs throughout their lives, and join the anti-drug movement anytime and anywhere. They should also tell their sons, mothers admonish their daughters, brothers encourage their younger brothers, and sisters encourage their younger sisters to make the whole family move to avoid being contaminated with opium and narcotic drugs and work hard. In this way, the family can be promoted to society, and it will be able to shake the power of smoke poison and fundamentally shake it. I hope that the female compatriots of our country will spread this goal and work hard to make the way to opium and other narcotic substance users is cut off. The opium, cultivation, transportation, and sale events that supply this need will also be cut off forever. (2) Organize a family anti-drug propaganda association. In everything, division leads to weakness and unity leads to strength. It is the same with the anti-drug movement. In order to achieve the goal, it is necessary to gather many like-minded people and carry out organized movements and conduct family anti-drug propaganda association for a united progress, so that women in general can: (1) understand the poison and harm of opium and narcotic drugs, and the family is the first to suffer. (2) Recognize that the anti-drug movement is a top priority, and strive to participate in the anti-drug movement to eradicate drugs and transform families. (3) Implement family anti-drug education, promote anti-drug health knowledge, investigate the real situation of family smoking disasters, and protect children from smoke poisoning. (4) Determine to refuse drugs and work together at any time and place to improve the family and eradicate drugs. Then the future of our country's anti-drug movement has great hopes.

Fourth Sheet>H]

Plan to Promote the Women's Anti-Drug Movement

The Chinese National Anti-Drug Association considers opium to be more devastating than raging floods and fierce beasts. The first to bear the brunt are families. Those addicted to smoking become mentally confused and abandon their proper occupations. Wealthy families easily become impoverished, and the poor are more likely to fall into despair. They pawn everything, neglecting their wives and children, leading to ruin, which is the first harm. With the family business ruined and daily sustenance difficult, the pain is exacerbated by the addictive nature of smoking. Driven to desperation, they resort to theft and deception, their character declines, and their morals are corrupted, which is the second harm. Once the smoking habit is deeply ingrained, the poison penetrates the bones, and it is passed down to future generations, causing endless harm, which is the third harm. Moreover, the sins are countless. Considering that women are essential members of the family, managing internal affairs and educating children, they occupy crucial positions in the home. Therefore, to restore family happiness and maintain family joy, it is especially important to promote the women's anti-drug movement. Once an anti-drug atmosphere is established in the home and anti-drug seeds are sown, no matter how cruel the drug is, what can it do to us? The Association has specifically formulated ten measures, inviting female compatriots across the country to promote and implement them, including: (1) Holding family anti-drug meetings, with local areas holding family anti-drug meetings organized and presided over by women; (2) Organizing family anti-drug propaganda teams, with local women's organizations and girls' schools forming family anti-drug propaganda teams to conduct door-to-door anti-drug propaganda; (3) Investigating the actual situation of family drug disasters, forming joint investigation teams to go to various places to investigate the actual situation of families tragically harmed by opium, leading to depravity; (4) Organizing children's anti-drug groups, with women's circles in various places initiating the formation of children's anti-drug groups, recruiting children from various families to join the publicity efforts and reject drugs for life; (5) Conducting written propaganda, with women's organizations in various places publishing anti-drug opinions in various newspapers from time to time, as well as works on the anti-drug movement and various women's issues; (6) Rejecting marriage with smokers, with women's circles and female students in various places uniting to form groups, vowing never to marry those who use drugs or are related to drugs, as a passive resistance; (7) Forming smoke paraphernalia destruction teams, with women in various places organizing groups of people, imitating the American women's temperance movement by chopping up wine tools and barrels, forming smoke paraphernalia destruction teams. For those who smoke at home, the smoking paraphernalia should be taken out and destroyed; (8) Holding anti-smoking petitions, with women's organizations in various places putting forward opinions on banning smoking, submitting them to local authorities, and requesting implementation; (9) Organizing women's anti-drug comradeships, uniting women from all walks of life, separately organizing women's anti-drug comradeships, and jointly seeking family improvement; (10) Promoting the sale of anti-drug monthly magazines, holding family anti-drug comrades meetings, and distributing them when investigating family drug situations in various places, while taking the opportunity to promote the sale of anti-drug monthly magazines.

Preparing for Anti-Drug Speech Competition. The Chinese National Anti-Drug Association holds a student anti-drug speech and essay competition once a year. This year, it was originally planned to be held during the anti-drug cycle, but due to the considerable time required for preparation, it was postponed. The Association's Education Department first formulated the speech competition regulations and rules, as well as the national essay competition regulations. It is reported that the speech competition, due to geographical reasons, will be held in Shanghai as well as in local branches in various provinces and cities. As for the essay competition, regardless of distance or field, anyone with considerable interest and research in anti-drug issues can submit their work. The Association announced various regulations yesterday, which are excerpted as follows: (A) "Student Anti-Drug Speech Competition Regulations" (1) Purpose: To promote anti-drug education, awaken the student community to study the scourge of opium and drugs, and jointly seek to eradicate them. (2) Scope: To be held within the county, divided into university, middle school, and primary school groups. All students, male or female, may participate. (3) Date and Location: To be determined at any time. (4) Speech Topics: Contestants from each school may choose their own topics, but they must be within the scope of anti-drug efforts. The speech topic must be submitted to the local anti-drug organization at the time of registration. All speeches must be delivered in Mandarin. (5) Number of Contestants: Each school is limited to one contestant. (6) Speech Time: Primary school students are limited to five minutes, middle school and university students are limited to ten minutes, and no extensions are allowed. (7) Judges: To be hired by the local anti-drug organization. (8) Judging Criteria: The judging criteria are divided into thought, structure, posture, and tone, with the following score distribution: (1, 2) each accounting for 30%, (3, 4) each accounting for 20%. (9) Awards: In addition to the Association's certificate, each locality will provide appropriate awards. The top three in universities and middle schools, and the top five in primary schools will be selected. If the winning speakers are able to record their speeches in vernacular Chinese and submit them to the Association for publication in the monthly magazine, they will receive a free half-year subscription to the Anti-Drug Monthly. (B) "Student Anti-Drug Speech Competition Rules" (1) Speech Order: The order of speeches will be determined by drawing lots. (2) Speech Time: University and middle school group speakers will each have a maximum of ten minutes. Primary school group speakers will each have a maximum of five minutes. (3) Timekeeping Standards: When university and middle school speakers reach nine minutes, and primary school speakers reach four minutes, the timekeeper will ring the bell once to notify them. When they reach ten minutes and five minutes respectively, the timekeeper will ring the bell twice. If the speaker has not finished, they should stop immediately after hearing the bell. (4) Judging Objectives: The judging objectives are divided into four categories: "Thought," "Structure," "Posture," and "Tone." The first two categories each account for 30%, and the last two categories each account for 20%, for a total of 100%. (5) Judging Criteria: The judges' judgment is the final decision of the competition, and no one has the right to object. However, those with opinions or statements can submit them to the Association's staff for transmission. (C) "Student Anti-Drug Essay Competition Regulations" (Purpose) To promote the student community's research on the scourge of opium and drugs and join the anti-drug movement. (Scope) People from all walks of life, regardless of gender, can participate in the scoring and division into "Essay," "Novel," "Play," and "Drawing" groups. (Topics) In addition to selecting from the topics proposed by the Association, participants may choose their own topics, but they must be within the scope of anti-drug efforts. (Format) Any literary style is acceptable, but each essay should not exceed 5,000 words. A list of reference books should be attached to the end of the essay. (Photo and Resume) A photo and resume, certified with the principal's signature and seal, must be sent along with the essay. (Judging Criteria) The judges will give marks according to the following points: (A) Accuracy of fact-finding, (B) Neatness of thought structure, (C) Conciseness and persuasiveness of writing. (Awards) In addition to the Association's certificates, appropriate awards will be determined locally. The top three in each group will be selected. In addition, all those who submit qualified essays and participate in the competition will receive a free half-year subscription to the Anti-Drug Monthly as encouragement.

Letter to Schools: Respected Sirs, the spread of opium is deeply entrenched, and its harm continues to escalate. This is a hidden concern for the nation and its people. Only by relying on the strength of the entire population can we carry out an eradication movement. The academic community is the backbone of society, and many support and promote the anti-drug movement. To arouse the academic community's interest in anti-drug efforts and to thoroughly eliminate drugs, the Association holds a speech competition once a year. It has been held for several sessions. This year, it was originally scheduled to be held during the national anti-drug cycle, but due to the complexity of affairs and the considerable time required for preparation, it was specifically postponed. The Association has stipulated the speech competition regulations and rules, as well as registration procedures. We hereby enclose the complete set and request that you check and collect them. We also ask that your school prepare to participate in order to achieve significant results. We earnestly pray for this. We deeply anticipate your reply. Sincerely, The Chinese National Anti-Drug Association.

Convening Joint Meeting of Bookstores

Regarding the inclusion of anti-drug materials in textbooks, the Chinese National Anti-Drug Association submitted a proposal to the First National Anti-Smoking Conference, which was passed. To implement this proposal, the Association plans to invite key personnel from major bookstores in Shanghai to hold a joint meeting to discuss implementation methods. It is reported that the measures it plans to submit to the joint meeting are as follows: (1) Send letters to bookstores across the country, according to the following principles, to include anti-drug teaching materials in primary and secondary school textbooks; (2) All textbooks that are compiled, reprinted, or newly compiled should immediately include the following teaching materials; (3) For textbooks that have already been published, supplementary teaching materials should be printed and attached to the book for supplementary teaching; (4) Civics textbooks: (A) In the hygiene section, the composition of opium should be analyzed in detail and how it affects physiology, so that students thoroughly understand that the harm of drug addiction is even greater than that of arsenic poisoning. Once committed, it will be harmful for life; (B) In the ethics section, in addition to explaining drug addiction, it is also appropriate to list examples of opium addicts who often indulge day and night, inhaling smoke and satisfying their addiction, often leading to laziness, career abandonment, and personality decline; (C) In the legal system section, add that those who indulge in opium and privately sell opium violate Article X of the criminal law and should be subject to legal sanctions; (D) In the economics section, in the family economics chapter, explain the methods of financial management, that smoking consumes a lot of money, and that a middle-class family can easily go bankrupt. Harming oneself is a small matter, but breaking the law and going bankrupt is even more serious. Good citizens should pay close attention to this. (1) Primary and secondary school history and geography textbooks should include anti-drug teaching materials. In addition to the original national education teaching materials, special attention should be paid to the meaning of anti-drug efforts so that students understand that the anti-drug movement is a form of patriotism; (2) Natural sciences: (A) In the botany aspect, the state, appearance, and nature of the poppy should be added; (B) In the chemistry aspect, the experiment of analyzing drug addiction should be added; (3) In the Chinese language section, select several of the best anti-drug essays written by doctors and have students study them, and have students write anti-drug essays.

Churches Unite Against Drugs. There are quite a few churches in the city. Yesterday, the Association sent personnel to carry various promotional materials to various churches for posting, and asked the churches to add anti-drug speeches during the worship service on the fifth day.

Statistics on Oaths. The Association pays great attention to anti-drug oaths every time it holds a campaign. During this anti-drug week, the Association plans to hold a national oath-taking ceremony. All printed materials include a type of oath form. According to the Association's statistics, during the three days, more than 3,000 representatives of the public in the city took oaths in person at various gatherings. According to the Association's statistics, 1,300 people in the city filled out oath forms and sent them to the Association in three days. Because the campaign only started three days ago, many oath forms from other places have not yet arrived. As of today, only about 800 copies have been counted.

Protest Against Inspection of Japanese Ship

The Japanese Qing Company's Luoyang Maru ship sailed from Hankou to Shanghai last month. When passing the Wusongkou, the Wusong Fortress Headquarters received a telegram in advance, knowing that bandits had boarded the ship in Jiujiang, posing as passengers, trying to mix into Shanghai. Therefore, it sent ten soldiers, taking a small boat to approach the ship, and advising it to stop entering the port and wait for inspection. After five minutes of searching, it would be allowed to sail to Shanghai. However, the Japanese shipowner believed that armed soldiers should not search Japanese merchant ships. After arriving in Shanghai, he immediately reported to the Japanese Deputy Representative Mitsuaki Kageyama. Yesterday (2nd), the Acting Consul General Mio Akio lodged a protest with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, demanding that sufficient attention be paid in the future to ensure that the same incident does not happen again.

Executive Committee Meeting of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

Fourth Session

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce held its fourth regular meeting of the Executive Committee at 4 p.m. yesterday. More than ten people attended, including Wang Xiaolai, Xu Jiyu, Zhu Wenqi, Lu Fengzhu, Gu Xinyi, Wu Zhihao, Fang Jiaobo, Chen Songyuan, and Lu Qiusheng. Chairman Wang Xiaolai presided over the meeting. After the formalities, Secretary Yan Esheng announced the resolutions of the third regular meeting, which were passed. After reporting on various letters, the following cases were discussed: (1) Discussion on the case of following the method of settling accounts according to the national calendar at the end of this year. First, the Secretary reported that the Association received a letter from the Hangzhou Municipal Cultural Association, stating that settling accounts at the end of the national calendar this year may be hindered. A flexible method was proposed to request an extension of one and a half months to solicit the Association's opinions. It was stated that following the national calendar is a national government order, and the government specially approved a one-month delay last year. It is impossible to request an extension this year. After detailed discussion by the members present, it was resolved that the settlement of accounts at the end of this year should be strictly in accordance with the national calendar. The Association will notify the industries to prepare in advance and announce to the southern part of the city to comply. (2) Discussion on the Association's finances. It was resolved to actively collect membership fees. The members will be responsible for persuading the guilds to pay the fees to the Association before the 15th of this month.

Work Relief Progress in Ninghai County, Shaoxing, Zhejiang

The Chinese Jiesheng Association previously received a letter from Sun Yinting, the Director of Work Relief in Ninghai County, Shaoxing, Zhejiang, reporting that the work relief for seawalls in Gudu, Xiadu, and Xuepo was progressing. During the heavy rain on the night of August 27, the three combined villages were flooded, causing 61 seawalls along the coast to collapse, damaging 13,000 mu of Ning rice, and affecting more than 5,000 people, cutting off their livelihoods. The Director inspected the work relief and calculated that the original budget needed to be increased threefold, which was previously reported. The Director carefully calculated again and again and reduced the number. Construction of the seawall and water storage cannot be done without tens of thousands of dollars. The Ningbo Ruiyu Zhuang Zhonghang has remitted 25,000 yuan for work relief. To complete the project, there is still a large difference. Work relief is different from emergency relief. If work relief is done well, there will be no floods and harvests can be abundant every year. It is really a win-win situation. At this moment of extreme urgency, good relationships should be established, and blessings will be immeasurable. This is what is expected of fellow philanthropists in Jiangsu and Zhejiang.

Inspection and Registration of Rice and Grain Will Be Handled by the Central Government

The Request to Set Up an Inspection Office in Jiangsu Province Was Rejected

The Municipal Government of this city previously received a report from the Shanghai County Government, stating that it was ordered by the province to establish a rice and grain inspection office in the city. It planned to find a suitable location in Nanshi and asked for filing and assistance. Since the registration of food transfer and export in this city has been handled by the Social Affairs Bureau and has been resolved by the Central Political Conference, the inspection and registration of food throughout the country should be handled by the Central Government in the future to unify authority. Therefore, should the proposal of the Shanghai County Government to set up an office in this city to inspect rice and grain be approved? After forwarding it to the Central Government for verification, the Executive Yuan forwarded it to the Ministry of Agriculture and Minerals for deliberation and reply, stating that the inspection and registration of food need not be entrusted to local agencies to unify authority. After receiving the order from the Municipal Government, the Secretariat has notified the Shanghai County Government for verification. The previous telegrams from various newspapers in this city, stating that the Shanghai Municipal Government's request to set up an inspection office was rejected, is a misunderstanding of this case.
